i < particleCount; i++) {\n      particles.push({\n        x: Math.random() * canvas.width,\n        y: Math.random() * canvas.height + 50,\n        vy: -(Math.random() * 0.4 + 0.1), // Slow upward drift\n        vx: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.15, // Subtle sway\n        radius: Math.random() * 1.5 + 0.5,\n        alpha: Math.random() * 0.3 + 0.1,\n        life: Math.random() * 100\n      });\n    }\n\n    const animate = () => {\n      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);\n      ctx.fillStyle = \"rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.4)\"; // Soft red glow particles\n\n      particles.forEach((p) => {\n        p.y += p.vy;\n        p.x += p.vx;\n        p.life -= 0.25;\n\n        // Reset particle if it drifts off screen or dies\n        if (p.y < -10 || p.life <= 0) {\n          p.x = Math.random() * canvas.width;\n          p.y = canvas.height + 10;\n          p.vy = -(Math.random() * 0.4 + 0.1);\n          p.vx = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.15;\n          p.life = Math.random() * 100 + 50;\n          p.alpha = Math.random() * 0.4 + 0.1;\n        }\n\n        // Pulse alpha gently\n        const currentAlpha = p.alpha * Math.sin((p.life / 100) * Math.PI);\n\n        ctx.beginPath();\n        ctx.arc(p.x, p.y, p.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n        ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(239, 68, 68, ${Math.max(0, currentAlpha)})`;\n        ctx.fill();\n      });\n\n      animationId = requestAnimationFrame(animate);\n    };\n\n    animate();\n\n    return () => {\n      window.removeEventListener(\"resize\", resize);\n      cancelAnimationFrame(animationId);\n    };\n  }, [showParticles, reducedMotion]);\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"absolute inset-0 w-full h-full overflow-hidden z-0 bg-black\">\n      {/* 1. Canvas Floating Particles */}\n      {showParticles && !reducedMotion && (\n        <canvas \n          ref={canvasRef} \n          className=\"absolute inset-0 z-30 pointer-events-none mix-blend-screen\"\n        />\n      )}\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n","Description":"Create components/intro/IntroOverlay.tsx with zooming background image, vignette, dark overlay, and slow canvas particles.","Overwrite":true,"TargetFile":"a:\\portfolio\\src\\components\\intro\\IntroOverlay.tsx","toolAction":"Creating IntroOverlay.tsx","toolSummary":"Create IntroOverlay.tsx"}}]}
